Havas, Geneva, 31st - The League of Nations Administrative Council, in accordance with the decision of the Lausanne Conference, appointed a committee to be responsible for the preparatory work for the World Economic Conference. This preparatory committee met this morning. First, the newly appointed Secretary-General of the League of Nations, Avenol, gave a welcome speech. Then, the committee elected Dr. Trip, the President of the Netherlands National Bank and a member of the International Clearing Bank Council, as the chairman of the committee. Trip explained the committee's task, which is to formulate an annotated agenda for the World Economic Conference. The committee also decided to organize two subcommittees, one for economic affairs and one for financial affairs. The preparatory committee will meet for approximately eight days to review various issues that can be included in the agenda of the Economic Conference, and then adjourn so that the members can seek opinions from their respective governments.

British House of Commons Questions Far East Matters 78

Reuters, London, 31st - The British Foreign Secretary stated in the House of Commons today in response to a question from Charlton of the Conservative Party that the Japanese government and the Manchurian authorities have both made concrete statements on maintaining the Open Door in Manchuria. The British government currently has no reason to doubt these statements. Charlton asked, "Can Sir Simon guarantee that there will be no restrictions in the future?" Simon replied, "We must proceed step by step. If there is no doubt that the Open Door policy is being maintained, then we can be satisfied." Regarding the claims from British merchants against the "Manchukuo" authorities for goods previously supplied, totaling £28,749, the matter is being reported by the British Commercial Counselor in Peiping. Regarding the recent wars in Shandong and Sichuan provinces within China, the lives and property of British nationals are still safe. The suppression of Communists in central and southern China is currently making good progress.

News Headlines

Japanese Public Opinion After the Report Was Published 79

After the League of Nations investigation report was published, the Japanese were outwardly furious and attacked the investigation team (and even the League of Nations) as much as possible. From attack to abuse, even stable and reasoned arguments must demand the withdrawal of Chapters 9 and 10 for a re-investigation. On the surface, Japan's national opinion is truly united and the country has a new-found spirit. But we have asked, examined closely, and investigated to find out that! There is still much doubt about the unanimity of public opinion. It turns out that before the League of Nations investigation report was published, Japan had a general understanding of its contents and had prepared early. The military stood at the front, calling for all subordinate organizations such as the "Reservist Association," the "Kokuhonsha," the "Black Dragon Society," the "Gyochi-sha" and other groups to prepare and mobilize together. When the report was published, the military sounded the alarm and instructed each division commander to mobilize the local reservists and the local newspapers to create a so-called unanimous public opinion. At the same time, it also brought up the "Manchukuo" puppet state it had built, using the name of "thirty million people" to launch a rebuttal to the report. What it calls public opinion is: (From the Asahi Shimbun to the Yorozu Chuoho and other magazines, they all adopted the same line.)

(1) They all expressed considerable goodwill towards the first chapter of the report, because it said that China was not yet a modern nation, and almost everyone quoted "It can be seen that China's internal division forces are still strong. The reason for this lack of unity is that most nationals only know family and township, but not the country, and only feel it slightly when the basic country is in a very tense diplomatic situation with other countries." The reason why they often quote this passage is to substantiate their claim that China has not formed a modern nation and can be arbitrarily invaded by militarism.

(2) They believe that from the League of Nations to the investigation team sent out by the League of Nations, they all lack practical knowledge of the past China and "Manchukuo," so the theories in the report are all empty talk on paper and have not actually touched the core of the problem. Therefore, they gave the report a verdict, calling it "insufficient understanding."

(3) Starting from this lack of understanding, the investigation team's judgment that the actions of the Japanese army, especially the military actions of September 18th, went beyond the scope of self-defense is unfair. As for believing that Japan harbors territorial ambitions and launches military aggression based on these territorial ambitions, it is even more of a misunderstanding among misunderstandings.

(4) Regarding the outbreak of the incident, the investigation team believed that Japan went beyond self-defense measures, and that the emergence of "Manchukuo" was not spontaneous, but was the activity of the Japanese army and officials. They even thought that this was slander, but they clearly stated the particularity of Manchuria (that is, Japan's special political and economic interests). They still think it's good.

(5) They all believe that the conditions and suggestions for resolution in Chapters 9 and 10 are violations of what they call the facts. This fact is the so-called independence of the puppet state, which has been recognized by Japan, and (armed) envoys have been sent. Therefore, they said, "The report is an empty theory, a travelogue, violates the facts, etc." Therefore, the Japanese government (which can simply be said to be the Japanese military) made opinions to the League of Nations based on the public opinion it created and based on the (puppet) public opinion it launched. The policy held by the Japanese representatives is:

"1. (The Japanese) Imperial Government's formal recognition of 'Manchukuo' is the serious execution of its national policy. No matter what situation is encountered, it will never revoke its recognition or (change) the nature of its recognition. Therefore, the discussions of the League of Nations must be carried out under the fact of (Japan's) recognition, with the non-movement of 'Manchukuo' independence as a prerequisite.

1. Impulsive resistance is enough to cause the worst situation, so it should naturally be avoided, and we should strive to do our best to coordinate in order to achieve a satisfactory solution. However, if (Japan's) legitimate claims are opposed to the League of Nations' claims and there is no room for compromise, then we should state the Empire's position and immediately and resolutely withdraw from the League of Nations.

2. (The Japanese) Imperial Government's views on the Lytton Report have been clearly stated in the opinions, and must be explained earnestly. That is, at the time of the Manchurian Incident, no matter what country faced it, it could not take any actions other than the actions taken by Japan. The League of Nations should fully understand this attitude."

This outline is certainly not enough to express Japanese public opinion, but it can express "imperial-made" public opinion, because the current Japanese newspapers and other periodicals are all dominated by the military's aggressive fanaticism, and there is nothing that can be found to be public opinion. Therefore, even people with a little clearer mind, such as Sasaki Hiroo, feel that it is too fanatical. Even Wax Mountain Seido felt that denying China's lack of a national organization as much as possible would result in "Manchukuo" not being truly independent (that is, it is tantamount to admitting that Manchukuo was made by Japan...) Isokaze Ichiro believes that Japan's recent freedom of speech is extremely narrow, and there seems to be no room for speaking. There is no way to say much, but he also saw clearly that the investigation team's report was woven into the complex relationships of international imperialism. Hosoda Tamiki believed that "the Lytton Report implies placing China under international joint management, especially 'Manchuria' must be divided fairly. Although the Japanese warlords view (the Lytton Report) as nothing more than an Asian travelogue, after all, in reality, it is a 'China Division Compass,' and the beginning of the great powers' division of China." Indeed, this statement seems a bit over the top, but he has insight into the psychology of imperialism. As far as Japan is concerned, since Uchida Yasuya (Foreign Minister) has gambled that "I (Japan) will fight for the Northeast even if it turns into scorched earth...", then all public opinion and all diplomatic maneuvers are useless. (October 24th, Tokyo)

Stalemate in the Sichuan War 80

Liu Wenhui Plans to Shorten Defense Lines and Take a Desperate Stand

Troops Hope Zhang Qun Will Enter Sichuan and Support Tian to Govern

Hankou Dispatch: The Sichuan War has been raging for a full month today. Initially, it was confined to Wusheng and Suining, then extended to Tongnan and Yongchuan, and finally, Chengdu was stained with blood, with corpses filling the city. The chaos is truly lamentable. When both sides issued general offensive orders, Liu Xiang seized the opportunity to occupy Wusheng, Suining, Tongnan, Yongchuan, and Jiangjin one after another. However, he later suffered some setbacks. In recent days, there has been no clear victor, so the original frontlines remain. Liu Wenhui, facing excessively broad defense zones and needing to balance various fronts, has decided to shorten the battle lines. The left wing will retreat to Anyue, the central wing to Dazu, and the right wing to Luzhou. If necessary, even Hechuan can be abandoned, concentrating all strength in Zizhong for a desperate last stand. In Chengdu, conflicts between Liu and Tian's troops have occurred twice. Under the armed surveillance of Deng Xihou, both sides are withdrawing their troops, with each stationing three regiments within the city. Tian's forces are stationed at the east, west, and north gates, Liu's forces at the south gate, and Deng's forces station over a division. In Jianyang, Tian and Deng's troops are stationed, with roughly equal strength, both isolating the two Lius and sharing the spoils. Other figures like Yang Sen and Liu Cunhou are also sending troops to grab a piece of the action, further complicating the Sichuan situation and making it even harder to resolve. According to insiders, this war was triggered by Liu Xiang's repeated confiscation of Liu Wenhui's weaponry. However, Liu Xiang's confiscation was not limited to the 24th Army. The weapons transported by Deng, Tian, Liu, and Yang were all confiscated when passing through Chongqing. The various armies have long resented Liu Xiang and wanted to deal with him, but they were unable to do so due to insufficient strength, daring to be angry but not daring to speak out. The generals advocate breaking up the defense zones, mainly because Liu Wenhui occupies the most territory, and everyone wants a share. They especially resent Liu Xiang's control of Chongqing. If Liu Wenhui had generously agreed to cede a dozen or twenty counties to Deng, Tian, and others to take over defense, then Deng and Tian would have certainly joined forces to attack Liu Xiang. Li, Luo, Liu, and Yang would also have risen up to support them. At the very least, they would have forced Chongqing to follow Chengdu's example, allowing various armies to station there. If that had happened, Liu Wenhui's losses would have been small, while Liu Xiang's losses would have been great. When Liu Wenhui opposed the Suining Conference, Liu Xiang instead expressed support, leading to dissatisfaction among the various armies towards Liu Wenhui, and they formed an alliance with Liu Xiang. However, although the generals are nominally allied with Liu Xiang, in reality, they are only outwardly compliant. Those directly fighting Liu Wenhui, apart from Li Jiayu and Luo Zezhou, are all directly subordinate to Liu Xiang. Deng, Tian, Liu, and Yang are not involved. Furthermore, Yang's deployment of troops was instigated by Liu Wenhui with 300,000 yuan. Deng's mediation is also aimed at withdrawing Chen Hongwen's division, creating a complex and unpredictable situation. Each is seeking a way out for themselves, and it is impossible for them to genuinely provide troops or support to any side. Currently, the two Lius are still fighting, and the final outcome depends on the actions of Deng, Tian, Liu, and Yang, with Deng and Tian having a particularly significant influence. It is said that there is a growing movement in Sichuan to force Liu Wenhui to hand over political power and support Tian Songyao as the chairman of the province. If this can be achieved, it may alleviate the situation and lead to a peaceful resolution. The generals are eagerly anticipating Zhang Qun's return to Sichuan. Liu Wenhui also does not oppose this, as Zhang is a Sichuan native, familiar with Sichuan affairs, has a position in the central government, and has connections with various parties. If he can offer suggestions, it will be easier to negotiate. Although Zhang has indicated that he will not go, he is studying ways to resolve the Sichuan situation and is rumored to be coming to Hankou soon to meet with Chiang Kai-shek to discuss everything. Perhaps after finding a solution, he will resolutely make the trip. (October 30)

Chongqing Air Dispatch: Since the Sichuan War began in Wusheng, Yu Liu (Xiang) and Rong Liu (Wenhui) only made formal contact in recent days. Fierce attacks and defenses have been taking place at Jiang (along the Yangtze River) and Yongchuan (on the Chengdu-Chongqing road). The Yu army (i.e., the 21st Army), led by Pan Wenhua and Mu Yingzhou, attacked Jiangjin, entering and exiting the city twice. Ultimately, with the assistance of the Yu side's air force and warships, a combined air, land, and sea attack forced the 24th Army's Xu Tingxiu brigade, which was defending the city, to withdraw completely from Jiangjin on the 27th. Both sides suffered significant losses in this battle, and nearly a hundred civilians in Jiangjin were killed by bombs dropped by Yu army planes.

On the land route to Yongchuan, the provincial army originally built five lines of strong defenses. After days of intense attacks by the Yu army and bombing by planes, the main defense lines were destroyed, and they retreated in disarray. The Yu army occupied Yongchuan City at 6:00 PM on the 27th.

After the formal contact between the 21st and 24th Armies, the fighting has become increasingly fierce, especially on the central Yongchuan front. The 21st Army is known for its firepower, while the 24th Army is known for its manpower. Each shows its special skills and pummels the other. After several days and nights of bloody fighting, the 21st Army finally prevailed after advancing and retreating three times. The situation on that front remains extremely tense. Liu Xiang personally led the police force to the front lines today to supervise the battle. At the same time, Chongqing has formally declared martial law due to the intense fighting on the front lines. (October 30)

Chairman Chiang's Tour of Hunan 81

Wanders Around Dongting Lake and Junshan Island While Passing Yuezhou

Visits Yue Lu Mountain to Pay Respects to the Four Martyrs After Arriving in the Province

Orders Commanders of Various Divisions Under He to Come to the Province for Instructions

Changsha Dispatch: When Chairman Chiang arrived in Hankou to direct the suppression of bandits, He Jian had repeatedly telegraphed, welcoming him to Hunan to give guidance. Due to busy military affairs, he had been unable to visit for a long time. On the afternoon of October 26th, Hu Xiehui, director of the 4th Route Army Office stationed in Hankou, telegraphed that the Commander-in-Chief was scheduled to come to Hunan on the afternoon of the 27th at 2 o'clock, accompanied by Madam Song and fourteen staff members, and a platoon of guards, aboard the Chu You and Wei Sheng warships, and would arrive in Changsha around noon on the 28th. Upon receiving the telegram, He Jian immediately sent section chiefs Su Yongqing and Luo Zhen, and liaison officer Peng Shufeng, to prepare for the welcome, and designated the Guan Yue Temple as the welcome preparation office. The entire Jin Lida Academy within the temple was used as Chiang's headquarters. The more than 300 students of the National Arts Training Institute, originally stationed in the academy, were moved to the provincial warehouse overnight. The Western-style building on the left front of the academy was used as Chiang's office, the rear room as the bedroom, the rooms on the right side as the male and female staff quarters, the room directly behind as the bathroom, the front room on the left downstairs as the staff room, the rear room as the chief of staff's office, the front room on the right as the code room, the rear room as the secretary-general's office, the room directly behind as the attendant's room, and the large flower hall upstairs in the Guan Yue Temple as the reception hall. All the rooms upstairs and downstairs in the headquarters were furnished with new Western-style furniture, brass beds, satin quilts, and carpeted floors, making them extremely clean and elegant. A notice was sent to all civil officials above section chief level and military officers above the rank of major, asking them to gather at the main wharf outside Xiaoximen at 10:00 AM on the 28th to welcome him. The entire Changjiang Hotel was temporarily rented as a rest stop for the welcoming party, and three small steamboats, Xinhongyun, Xinhongtai, and Xinchangjiang, were rented to go out to meet the warships when they arrived. He Jian also sent Huang Fei, director of the Aviation Bureau, to fly downstream to meet him. By noon, several hundred party, government, and military officials, led by He Jian, had gathered at the Changjiang Hotel to wait. At 12:30 PM, Huang Fei returned to the province by plane and reported that the Chu You and Wei Sheng warships were still anchored in Yuezhou and that no warships had sailed upstream from Yueyin, indicating that Commander-in-Chief Chiang was still staying in Yuezhou. At the same time, Duan Heng, commander of the garrison brigade in Yuezhou, also telegraphed that Chairman Chiang had arrived in Yuezhou at 12:00 PM and was touring Dongting Lake and Junshan Island with Madam Song, and that he would set sail for Changsha from Yuezhou at around 3:00 PM. Chiang also telegraphed He Jian from Yuezhou at that time, saying that he was scheduled to leave Yuezhou for the province at 4:00 PM and would arrive around 10:00 PM, asking him to inform all parties not to welcome him and that he would not attend a banquet. So the welcoming party temporarily dispersed and decided to gather again at 10:00 PM that evening to welcome him. When the time came, several hundred people gathered on the riverbank for the second welcome. They waited until 11:00 PM without seeing him. Just as everyone was anticipating his arrival, they received another telegram from Duan Heng in Yuezhou, saying that the Commander-in-Chief had finished visiting Junshan Island at 3:00 PM and had transferred to the Jiangkun warship to sail to the province, but due to the shallow water, he had to stop sailing at night and would arrive in the province around 2:00 PM on the 29th. So the second welcoming party dispersed again. By about 1:00 PM on the 29th, party, government, and military leaders, as well as the public, gathered again at the main wharf outside Xiaoximen to welcome him. At 1:50 PM, the Jiangkun warship arrived at the port, military music played in unison, and He Jian and others boarded a small boat to welcome Chairman Chiang and his wife ashore, and they rode in cars directly to the Guan Yue Temple for a welcoming banquet. During the banquet, Chiang declared that this trip was purely for touring purposes and had no other tasks. He also said that since the 31st was the anniversary of the death of the Hunan martyrs Huang (Xing), Cai (E), Jiao (Dafeng), and Chen (Zuo Xin), he had decided to go to Yue Lu Mountain on that day to pay respects to the martyrs and to admire those who had gone before. If time permitted, he would also visit Heng Mountain in Nanyue. He Jian and Liu Jianxu then asked him if they could telegraph the commanders of the various divisions of the Fourth Route Army to come to the province to listen to his instructions. Chiang asked how many days it would take to gather everyone, and He said about four or five days. Chiang then agreed. He Jian immediately telegraphed five division commanders, Wang Dongyuan, Peng Weiren, Li Jue, Tao Guang, and Chen Guangzhong, ordering them to set off immediately for the province to hear instructions. This indicated that Chiang would stay in Hunan for four or five days. Chiang and his staff members decided to stay at the Guan Yue Temple headquarters, but Madam Chiang, finding the headquarters inconvenient, moved to He Jian's residence on Zhongshan Road. (October 29)

Situation of the Zhengtai Railway Takeover 82

Shijiazhuang Dispatch: The Zhengtai Railway takeover issue, which has been rumored for over a year, has recently become a reality. Here is a record of the entire process:

The Zhengtai Railway was built with a loan in the 28th year of Emperor Guangxu of the Qing Dynasty, and thirty years have passed since then. The principal and interest on the loan have been repaid, and the operating contract expired on October 15th. In addition to the chairman of the takeover committee, Wang Maogong, and the takeover members Zhu Hua, Luo Yingjun, Wang Tairui, and Wu Renfu, who arrived at the railway bureau earlier to prepare for the takeover in accordance with the Ministry of Railways' order, the Ministry of Railways recently sent counselor Ling Ji and specialists Yang Nian and Li Dan to supervise and assist in handling all takeover matters. After consultation between Chairman Wang and the French deputy chief engineer, it was decided to hold a takeover ceremony on October 25th, followed by a separate inventory. Once the entire inventory is completed, both parties will sign, and the takeover procedures will be completed. The takeover ceremony was held in the railway staff association hall. More than thirty representatives from all parties and guests attended, as well as more than two hundred people, including middle-level staff of the railway, union representatives, and French staff. The meeting opened at 9:00 AM on the 25th. First, Wang Maogong, director of the railway bureau and chairman of the takeover committee, presided over the meeting and performed the necessary formalities. Then, the chairman invited the French deputy chief engineer and the Ministry of Railways' supervisors to speak. Next, guests spoke, including Huang Shiyue, commander of the 17th Brigade, Pan Lianru, representative of Yan Xishan, director of the Taiyuan Pacification Office, Zhang Yongchi, chairman of the Shimen Chamber of Commerce, Cao Lingxiao, chief of staff of the 17th Brigade, Liu Yunlu, director of the Shimen Public Security Bureau, Zhou Zhongli, representative of the Pinghan Railway, Qi Houzhi, representative of the Shanxi Provincial Government, Shi Fengxiang, director of the Daxing Yarn Factory, Liu Bingyi, instructor of the Shimen Industrial Zone, Chen Yaoxian, magistrate of Huolu County, and Zhang Lianhui, chief inspector representing the Shanxi Zhengtai Police Bureau. Wang Fengshu, a member of the Zhengtai Union Standing Committee, spoke on behalf of the staff, expressing congratulations and expectations for the takeover of the railway. The ceremony concluded at 11:00 AM. After taking a group photo, the railway staff accompanied the guests and French staff to the Zhengtai Hotel for lunch. They dispersed happily at 1:00 PM in the afternoon. The railway authorities plan to collect all relevant materials and publish a commemorative album to mark the takeover and remind themselves not to forget the past, and to be vigilant.

Resolution of the Anhui Salt Affairs Revision Dispute 83

Wuhu Dispatch: The Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office changed its regulations, ordering all shops engaged in the sale of edible salt to provide guarantees to obtain licenses and to submit a four-column list of daily salt sales for inspection. All salt shops in the province objected, arguing that providing guarantees was unprecedented and that daily reporting was cumbersome and practically impossible. Moreover, before these regulations were implemented, salt shipments from various places were already being detained and fined by tax police for slight delays. As a result, letters and telegrams were exchanged, and opposition was widespread. The Anhui Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce, at the request of local chambers of commerce, telegraphed the Ministry of Finance's Salt Affairs Administration, requesting that the Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office be ordered to continue operating under the old regulations to avoid disturbances. It is now reported that Wuhu's chief magistrate, Gao Shouheng, mediated the matter for several days, and the Inspection Office has accommodated the salt shops' requests and made changes. A dispute has been resolved. The Provincial Federation of Chambers of Commerce received a notice from Magistrate Gao yesterday and has notified the local chambers of commerce. The points of resolution are recorded below: (1) Regarding the issue of providing guarantees to obtain licenses, the merchants proposed that licensed merchants would definitely comply with the regulations, but guarantees were unprecedented and reputable merchants would not want to bear this heavy responsibility for others. The resulting solution was that a shop with two businesses could guarantee itself, without being overly demanding. (2) Regarding the issue of submitting daily reports, the merchants proposed that the procedures were too cumbersome, and any discrepancies would be rejected. Moreover, most shops also sold general merchandise and could not afford to hire additional staff to handle salt affairs specifically. The resulting solution was that a notice has been issued to change the reporting frequency to once a month. (3) Regarding the issue of fines for late salt shipments, the merchants proposed that salt shipments to various ports were transported by sailboats, and if they encountered wind, rain, or unexpected events en route, they would be punished regardless of the circumstances, only considering whether the deadline was exceeded, causing unbearable hardship. The resulting solution was that there was a notice in place stating that the deadlines would be enforced realistically and that circumstances would be taken into account. (4) Regarding the issue of harassment by tax police, the merchants proposed that tax police in various ports were taking advantage of the situation to harass merchants and arbitrarily cause trouble. They requested that this be prohibited to stabilize business. The resulting solution was that harassment by tax police would be strictly prohibited, and any complaints would be investigated and dealt with according to the evidence. (30th)

Proceedings of the 8th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Meteorological Society 84

The Chinese Meteorological Society held its 8th Annual Meeting on the 30th of last month at the library of the Meteorological Research Institute on Beijige in the capital. Over thirty members attended, with members from Jinan and Nantong rushing to Beijing to attend. Dr. Gao Lu, a director, made a special trip from Shanghai to attend. The meeting opened at 9:00 AM, and the necessary formalities were performed. First, Dr. Zhu Kezhen, president of the society, reported that Vice President Jiang Bingran had telegraphed to explain why he could not attend. Then, he delivered an opening speech, discussing "The Progress of the Meteorological Community Worldwide in the Past Year" and highlighting two important endeavors: (1) The Implementation of the International Polar Year observation plan, during which a total of sixteen countries sent ships to explore the North and South Poles starting in August of this year. Our country also sent personnel from the Meteorological Research Institute of the Academia Sinica to establish observation stations on Mount Tai and Mount Emei. (2) The Measurement of Cosmic Rays, in which Professor Piccard from Belgium conducted a second high-altitude expedition, ascending over 10,000 meters to measure the phenomena of the stratosphere. Finally, he discussed the recent situation of meteorological construction in various provinces of our country. After President Zhu's speech, Secretary-General Zhuge Qi reported on the progress of the society's affairs over the past year and the financial situation of editing the society's journal. Then, Mr. Gao Lu gave a speech on "Recent Specialized Work in Meteorology," divided into three sections: (1) The Position of Meteorology, (2) Meteorological Research in China, and (3) International Meteorological Research. Member Liu Weiqing also spoke on the importance of long-term forecasting. Then, papers were read (Liu Zengmian on the winds of Jinan in the past fourteen years, Liu Zhihua on local weather forecasting methods, Zheng Zizheng on changes in the climate of Beijing, Zhu Wenrong on upper-level air currents and weather in Nanjing, and Zhu Binghai on the condensation nuclei of fog). At noon, everyone had lunch together at the meteorological station and took a group photo to commemorate the event. The meeting continued at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, and seven new members were introduced. Then, Nanjing was elected as the location of the secretariat, Zhu Kezhen was elected as president, Jiang Bingran as vice president, and Chen Zhanxue, Liu Zhihua, Shen Xiaofeng, Liu Enlan, Zhu Wenrong, Xu Yingqi, Gao Jun, and Zheng Zizheng as directors, with Zhuge Qi as secretary-general. After the elections, proposals were discussed. By 6:00 PM, the Meteorological Research Institute hosted a banquet. The following are excerpts of the important cases passed: (1) A letter will be sent to the construction departments of various provinces to request that affiliated meteorological stations increase upper-air meteorological observations. (2) Since meteorological reports are related to national defense, it is proposed that the society consult with the Academia Sinica to convene a meeting of relevant departments to discuss restriction methods. (3) A letter of condolence will be sent in the name of the conference to Father Laborie of the Xujiahui Observatory for his meritorious service. (4) Meteorological agencies should focus on studying long-term forecasting. (5) A petition will be submitted to the Executive Yuan to order all provinces to establish a first-class meteorological station within a time limit. (6) It is requested to promote the study of advanced meteorology. (7) A letter will be sent to the Ministry of Interior and the Meteorological Research Institute of the Academia Sinica to implement an investigation of the performance of meteorological stations in various regions.

Taicang 85

▲Public Security Sub-Bureau Continues to Capture Thieves The Shuangfeng Public Security Sub-Bureau's jurisdiction had two robbery cases last month, and they immediately launched a strict investigation and arrest operation, capturing the robbers of Yang Xiong and Wu Zigeng's families, Yan Baochi and Wu Zhongmei. They have already been sent to the county and sentenced to seven years in prison. On the 26th of last month, Wang Alian was also captured. Songjiang 86

▲Songjiang, Fengxian, and Shanghai-South Boundary Delimitation Conference The various townships and towns east of Yexie Pond along the Punan border of this county, such as Zhaolin, Chongque, Hujiaqiao, and the 14th district area, Fengxian proposed that they should be placed under Fengxian's jurisdiction, while the various townships in Fengxian bordering Nanhui should be transferred to Nanhui. The case was submitted to the Ministry of Civil Affairs for approval. After being instructed to inform this county to reply, various local sectors, upon hearing of the matter, sent numerous letters and telegrams, advocating opposition. The case was suspended due to the sudden outbreak of the Shanghai War. The delimitation of the Shanghai-South border was also not implemented. It has recently been reported that the various counties have re-submitted the old case. After negotiation and decision, a joint conference of county government and commercial representatives will be held on the 11th of this month at the 8th floor of the Huaan Life Insurance Company on Jing'an Temple Road in Shanghai. At that time, the relevant county magistrates will participate in the meeting with local impartial gentry and merchants. Shen Yong, the county magistrate of this county, believes that this case involves boundary issues and is very important. He is currently carefully selecting impartial gentry in order to represent and participate in the meeting. Fengxian County was originally carved out of the former Huating County. How can the people of Songjiang be willing to hear Fengxian's desire to carve out Songjiang? It is expected that there will be a dispute at the Shanghai conference.

Wuxi 87

▲Four-County Joint Defense Zone Conducts Joint Patrols The Four-County Joint Defense Zone of Wuxi, Wujin, Chengjiang, and Yushan held its 11th joint defense conference at the county government of this county the day before yesterday. The chairman was Chen Chuande, the magistrate of Wuxi County. The items discussed were: (1) Most of the counties in this joint defense zone are bordered by rivers and lakes, with numerous branching waterways. Sampans and fishing boats are constantly traveling back and forth, and it is difficult to ensure that there are no bandits hiding. It is proposed to order the various district offices along the rivers and lakes to drive wooden stakes into the less important small ports to prohibit passage. The major ports will be ordered to be carefully searched by the police at any time. It was decided that the various joint defense zones should deliberate and implement the measure. (2) As the winter defense season is approaching, it is imperative to supervise the implementation of joint patrols. The six measures decided upon are as follows: A. During the winter defense period, joint patrols will be conducted twice a month. The dates and locations will be determined separately. B. Irregular joint patrols may be conducted at any time by either side based on the border situation. C. When police and security agencies in the joint defense counties are ordered to conduct joint patrols, the respective commanders should jointly implement them. D. The joint patrol certificates should be exchanged during the joint patrol, and the joint patrol situation should be attached to the certificates and forwarded to the respective county governments for verification. E. The joint patrol certificates will be issued by the four-county joint defense office. F. Those who fail to attend scheduled joint patrols without good reason will be punished by their respective agencies. (3) The duration of each defense period was decided to be from November 1st to March of next year. (4) The wandering soldiers and scattered troops staying in the townships and towns will be expelled. (5) Tea houses and hotels in the townships will be investigated for harboring travelers. (6) The date of the next meeting was set for 2:00 PM on November 26th and will still be held at the Wuxi County Government. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

▲Party Headquarters Investigates Opium Public Sale The rumor of the public sale of opium in Jiangsu Province is rampant, with everyone talking about it, but the authorities are still vehemently denying it. Recently, the rumor of public sale in this county has become more prevalent, and there is even talk of Xuan Junhou contracting the two counties of Wuxi and Yixing. The various members of the 1st District Party Headquarters believed that this matter had been repeatedly denied by the provincial government, but it has been mentioned so frequently and with such certainty in newspapers and society that there must be some basis for it. Therefore, at the 18th committee meeting held yesterday, a proposal was put forward, based on the Premier's admonition against drugs, to request the superior party headquarters to conduct a strict investigation. At the same time, in view of the urgent need for anti-Japanese forces in the Northeast, and the lack of fighter planes, it was decided to request the county assembly to organize a national salvation movement to raise funds for national defense aircraft, and to conduct fund-raising activities in various ways.

Jiangyin 88

▲Tragic News of a Jiangyin River Boat Sinking a Pig Boat Yongxing Pig Firm in Longwo Town, Taixing, previously received a letter from Li Runzhi at No. 2 Xuejiabang Youchelong in Shanghai, ordering 129 pigs, scheduled to be shipped to Shanghai. On the 29th, boatman Cao Jinhai loaded the pigs, along with more than a dozen passengers from Jiangbei, and sailed to the Sidunzi area. At around 8:00 PM, a certain river boat (some say it was a Japanese boat, others say it was a Sanbei Company boat) sailing downstream suddenly crashed into the boat, splitting it in two. People and pigs all sank into the river. Boatman Cao was drowned. Yesterday morning (30th), a Jiangjing rescue ferry sailed to the scene of the accident and salvaged the two halves of the boat, 44 dead pigs, 2 live pigs, and the bodies of six people, including boatman Cao Baoer. The Suhang Pig Industry Association telegraphed Taixing and Shanghai. Yongxing Pig Firm immediately sent Cai Dequan to Cheng to handle everything that evening.

▲Truck Hits and Injures Soldier A truck with license plate Jing Zi No. 1703, loaded with stones, was driving east-west at around 10:00 AM yesterday. When it reached the entrance of the Da Dong Barber Shop on Shanxiangdi Xinmalu, the driver, Ding Xuchang, saw an old woman coming towards him. He swerved to avoid her, but unfortunately, Private Yin Yongsheng of the 9th Squad of the Cavalry Company of the Security Department was passing by and was unable to dodge in time. He was knocked to the ground, and his left ankle was crushed by the truck. The stones on the truck also fell, injuring Yin's genitals. The police officer on duty, Fu Sheng, witnessed the incident and had Yin taken to Sirene Hospital for treatment. He also took the truck driver, Ding Xuchang, to the 2nd Precinct and then transferred him to the 3rd Bureau for investigation.

Pinghu 92

▲ Basic Squad Captures Four Bandits: After the bandits in the eastern countryside were dispersed by the army, the remnants, led by Cai Xian, Shen Jin, and Shen, resurfaced recently. They kidnapped the grandmother of Yao Zhiming in Xinmiao Town, demanding a ransom of 200,000 yuan. After the victim asked people to negotiate several times, they recently agreed on 24,000 yuan and were about to redeem her. However, Shen Jin, the bandit leader, had the intention of washing his hands and surrendering last month. He sent a letter to Gan Kaijun, the captain of the basic squad, offering to reform himself and release the Yao hostage to atone for his past sins. On the 27th, he ordered his concubine, Wang Yahua, and fellow villager, Huang Kechang, to come to Pinghu from Shanghai and agree on the date of the ransom with Captain Gan. After replying to Shen Jin, he again ordered his concubine, Wang Yahua, and a small bandit, Shen Baolin, to go to Jiangzhuang in Songjiang County to inquire about the hostage from Cai Shenglai, the bandit in charge. While they were talking, the basic squad suddenly arrived. Shen Baolin, feeling guilty, quickly escaped. Wang Yahua and Cai Sheng were arrested and taken to Xincang for interrogation. Wang confessed that her husband, Shen Jin, instructed her to contact Cai Laoban and release the hostage, then go to the Datong Inn in Pinghu to meet him for surrender. After interrogating Cai, he refused to confess anything. Captain Gan Kaijun ordered Secretary Hu Zhengyue to lead a part of the militia to go to Pinghu to wait. Shen arrived as expected, using the alias "Lu" and staying at the Datong Inn. Hu immediately ordered the militia to surround the area and capture Shen. On the night of the 30th, the four bandits were escorted to the basic squad headquarters of the county security regiment, detained overnight, and escorted to the county government yesterday for review. Efforts are currently being made to rescue the Yao hostage.

Special Education News

A Relatively Scientific Teaching Guidance Plan (1) Du Gang 97

The meaning of teaching guidance is very complex. Analyzed, it can be divided into the following three aspects: (1) Generally, teaching guidance is nothing more than the inspection of the teaching situation in schools, such as teaching equipment, teaching methods, teachers' and students' activities, and other conditions that can improve teaching efficiency. This is the most basic meaning of teaching guidance. However, in China, it seems already commendable if teaching guidance can be done thoroughly. (2) Teaching guidance is considered to be the training of teachers in service, so that teachers can expand their educational knowledge, improve their educational skills, and encourage their spirit of service. This meaning is undoubtedly more advanced, because according to this meaning, the instructor is not only an inspector but also needs to gain the trust and cooperation of teachers and assist teachers in improving their teaching. Therefore, the scope of teaching guidance is also more extensive. (3) The purpose of teaching guidance is to improve all aspects of teaching, such as defining mathematical goals, selecting and organizing teaching materials, arousing motivation, adapting to individuality, guiding learning, and other teaching methods, as well as physical conditions such as indoor temperature, light, ventilation, and seating. Here, the meaning of teaching guidance is more advanced and more extensive. The instructor is not only a teaching inspector or a teacher trainer but also an educational research expert responsible for improving all aspects of teaching. The above three aspects of the meaning of teaching guidance can also be said to be the three stages of the expansion of the meaning of teaching guidance. In the United States, the practice of teaching guidance has almost progressed to the third stage, while in China, it still remains in the first stage. Therefore, how to increase the efficiency of teaching guidance and how to change the aspects of teaching guidance is indeed a current question for China's educational administration. Based on the author's usual observations, teaching guidance in the future should strive from the following aspects:

Ministry of Education Sends Personnel to Shanxi for Inspection 98

▲ Observations on Education in Shanxi by Yu Tan

Taiyuan Correspondence: In order to inspect education in various provinces in North China, the Ministry of Education specially dispatched supervisors Yu Senwen and Dai Xia, who came to Shanxi together on the 22nd for on-site inspection. The Education Department sent personnel to receive them, and they stayed at the Jingu Xiang Hotel. The next day, they inspected Shanxi University and various colleges and universities in Bingyuan. They are expected to inspect for six days in Bingyuan, and then Dai will go to various counties in northern Shanxi, while Yu will go to southern Shanxi and then to Shaanxi for inspection. Mr. Yu talked to reporters about the schedule of inspecting education in various places, the future educational policies set by the Ministry, and his observations on education in Shanxi. The details of his talk are recorded as follows:

According to the talk, the school scale in Shanxi is grand and the buildings are complete. The biggest regret is the lack of books in the Faculty of Arts and Law and the lack of complete practice factories in the Faculty of Engineering. This is due to the lack of economy. The simple habits of poor students are rare in national universities. The spirit of the students is especially commendable. However, when we (Yu and Dai) asked the students to find the latest published books, the school had the least. The students' thinking can be known roughly from this. This is also caused by the environment in which they are located. Next, he said that the purpose of this inspection is to have a whole clear understanding of the situation of middle schools, universities, and primary schools in China, and to make a real survey and plan. Therefore, when leaving, seven outlines were prepared in advance: (1) Publicize the central education policy; (2) Supervise the implementation of the Ministry's programs; (3) Investigate the efficiency of local education administration; (4) Review the allocation and use of education funds; (5) Investigate and guide the facilities of education at all levels and social education; (6) Investigate the academic style and moral education situation; (7) Assess the performance of school personnel. He also talked about Shanxi University, which was jointly investigated by us (Yu) and Supervisor Dai. It was originally planned to be completed on the morning of the 22nd. Later, because the high school department of the school was combined with various colleges, it was completed together. On the 22nd, they saw the experimental primary school. In the afternoon, they went to the Education Department for inquiries. The 23rd was Sunday, and they took the opportunity of the school's holiday to visit Jinci Temple and returned to Bingyuan in the evening. The principals of various schools are invited to take the opportunity to talk about the precautions that schools should pay attention to in school. On the 24th, they went to Fenyang together to inspect middle and primary schools. On the 25th, Supervisor Dai went to the northern Shanxi area to inspect the middle and primary schools along the motor road, planning to stay in Zhe County for one day, in Jingle County for two days, in Dai County for two days, in Dingxiang for one day, in Datong for four days, in Lingqiu for one day, in Pingding for two days, and in Taiyuan City for five days. We (Yu) and Supervisor Dai divided the inspection. We (Yu) inspected the Faculty of Law, the School of Agriculture, the Business School, the Provincial No. 1 Women's Normal School, and the Provincial No. 1 Middle School, as well as Chengcheng Middle School. Dai inspected the College of Education, the Engineering School, the Bingzhou University, the No. 1 Normal School, the National Normal School, the Private Guanghua Women's Middle School, and three primary schools, as well as Bingzhou Middle School and Xinmin Middle School. Dai went to the north, and we (Yu) began to inspect the schools to be inspected. After we finished the inspection in Taiyuan, we went to the south to inspect the primary schools along the motor road, planning to stay in Qixian for one day, in Pingyao for one day, in Linfen for three days, in Zhaocheng for two days, in Xinjiang for one day, in Wenxi for one day, and in Yuncheng for three days. After the completion, he went to Shaanxi on the Longhai Line. On the one hand, he inspected various schools in Chang'an, and on the other hand, he was ordered to give special guidance to education in Shaanxi. Supervisor Dai returned to Bingyuan from the north, and then inspected the schools assigned to him. After the Taiyuan affairs were completed, Dai took the inspection results of various schools and took the Zhengtai car to Pinghan and returned to Beijing to report.

▲ Teachers, Students, and Alumni Sacrifice and Cooperate to Revive

After the accidental fire in the building in the second district of the Junior High School Department of Jiangsu Provincial Yangzhou Middle School, classes at all levels continued as usual, and students' studies were not affected. The Education Department sent a section chief to Yangzhou yesterday to investigate in detail and learned that all the reports of the school were true. The loss this time amounted to 20,000 yuan for both public and private parties. The fire was caused by street light electricity, which was not preventable by human power. However, all the faculty and staff of the school specially held a meeting yesterday to discuss the issue of revival. Yesterday, a reporter went to visit Mr. Zheng Xigu, the former principal of the school, about the dispute between the Huangdu Local Security Regiment and the Provincial Rural School. Mr. Zheng gave a detailed explanation. His talk is recorded above: "Huangdu Rural Normal School was changed to the Rural Normal Department of Shanghai Middle School in the summer of the 16th year of the Republic of China. In the autumn of this year, the Education Department stipulated that rural normal schools in the province should be independent. The Huangdu Rural Normal School was succeeded by the original director, Mr. Teng Songshi, as the principal. Mr. Teng is full of educational knowledge and experience, sincere and responsible, and highly trusted by all the faculty and staff and students of the school. After the trial implementation of work-study experimental education last autumn, all the teachers and students of the school were able to work together with one heart and one mind to strive for the experiment of new education. And the people of Huangdu have always cooperated with the school, and they have given a lot of support to the work-study primary school. Unexpectedly, the security regiment and the school recently had a dispute. This is a very unfortunate event. However, the process of this matter has been stated by all the students of the rural normal school in the newspaper. The students' statement is indeed true. On the 25th of last month, I accompanied the Section Chief of the Education Department to the Rural Normal School for inspection. There was no opposition in the school, and they were very trusted. At that time, all the students were very angry with the behavior of the security regiment. Later, the deputy regiment leader of the regiment, Mr. Zhang, came to the school to apologize and promised to be responsible for the security of the school in the future. This dispute was resolved immediately. In the past five years, the rural normal school has gained the support and encouragement of the local people. In the future, it is hoped that they will continue to support the school with the original intention of protecting the rural normal school. Not only will the new education experiment of the rural normal school be realized, but also the local cause can receive indirect promotion and effect."

Memorial Service for Female Educator Zhu Xuejing 103

Ms. Zhu Xuejing (courtesy name Danru), the wife of Mr. Zhang Zhongbin, was one of the few female educators in the country. Unfortunately, she passed away this summer, which is deeply regrettable. Colleagues in the education field held a memorial meeting at the auditorium of Shanghai Provincial Middle School at 2:00 PM on the 30th of last month. For a time, teachers, friends, and students came in plain cars and white horses, and there were as many as seven or eight hundred wreaths and elegies. At 2:00 PM, the meeting was opened with mournful music and salutes. After a moment of silence to pay tribute, Chairman Zheng Xigu gave a speech, followed by female students from Shanghai Middle School offering wreaths. Mr. Zhang Lunqing represented the attendees and read the eulogy. Mr. Cai Yishun represented Principal Zheng of the Women's Sericulture School and all the teachers and students to read the eulogy. Guests He Bingsong, Ren Mengxian, Zhang Xian, Zhu Jing'an, Tian Ding'an, Gu Defang, and Zhu Fanglin gave speeches one after another, expressing their deep condolences, respect, and regret. Finally, Mr. Zhang Zhonghuan, a family member, gave a thank-you speech. The meeting ended after 5:00 PM. Ms. Zhu devoted herself to education for nearly 20 years, being calm and dignified, and without any of the habits of the present. Since she married Mr. Zhang, she has been able to serve the school on the one hand and handle family affairs on the other. The couple respected and encouraged each other and worked together on the cause of education. This summer, she died of an accident during childbirth, which is a pity not only for the women in our country but also a loss of talent for the education field in our country. It is said that the lady was good at Chinese studies, and there are still one volume each of poetry and prose collections. Mr. Zhang will soon print and publish them for the world.

Weng Zhaoyuan Farewell Meeting, Scout Ensemble "Unifying the Mountains and Rivers" 104

Yesterday, all sectors of the city convened a meeting to bid farewell to Weng Zhaoyuan. The Scout of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce ensemble military music, the tune name Unifying the Mountains and Rivers. This tune is composed of ancient Chinese musical instruments, referring to foreign tunes. The large and small instruments are originally divided into four types of blowing, striking, pulling, and playing, totaling 66 pieces. Yesterday, because some of the scouts did not arrive, only half of them were used. The leader of the regiment, Ye Chunnian, and the deputy leader, Xu Guozhi, personally guided. The names of the musical instruments are recorded as follows: marching drum, staff drum, nagger, square sound, copper drum, nao, cangqing, star, jiena, tuba, double four-pipe, star, bugle, pan flute, head pipe, Yizhi Liu, Hailiu, large and small hurley, zither, Labpa, violin, piano, etc.

Two Points Victory, Hujiang Breaks the Pirates 109

Thirty-eight to Thirty-six Points

A Basketball Battle in Yangshupu

丨 Aid the Northeast Righteous Army丨

The Hujiang University basketball team defeated the Xiqing Pirates team, which has been dominating the sea for many years, by two points last night. The result was thirty-eight to thirty-six. The basketball stadium of the school in Yangshupu was crowded with people, mostly male and female students of the school. The proceeds from the ticket sales will be remitted to the Northeast to help the Righteous Army. Peng Sanmei executed the referee.

Hujiang Is Not Perfect. Hujiang's performance cannot be said to be disappointing, but it is not yet perfect. The cooperation skills seem to be improved. In the first ten minutes of the game, both sides were extremely panicked. Only people and horses were running around and bumping into each other blindly. After the people gradually calmed down, the ball situation suddenly became stagnant. The lack of preparation for shooting is the most disappointing. The opponent committed seven fouls, and only Feng Nianhua made two points. Among the forwards, Feng is still the most commendable, and the guards are average. At the beginning of the season, it is impossible to ask too much. You must know that the opponent is a strong enemy.

Pirates Are Always Terrible. Last night can be said to be one of the most subdued nights for the Pirates. The difference in throws under the basket was sixteen points. The number of hits is not satisfactory. Smith only hit two balls, which can be said to be a big deal. The reason is that the unfamiliarity of the field is one, and the four corners of the field are too low, so those who are not accustomed to it cannot shoot. Hujiang is not as fast as Hujiang in dribbling. There are more opportunities than Hujiang. The failure to hit is also due to the poor luck. The strength is terrible, and it cannot be taken lightly because of this defeat.

The Situation on the Court Is Tense. When the game started, the ball situation was fast and extremely tense. Smith first hit after a chaotic battle. Hujiang surpassed with eight to three. The Pirates tied with ten to ten. Unfortunately, Da Shigiya was slightly injured and out due to Sun Baoqing's collision. Xiqing was punished instead, so he showed shaking, but still maintained a tie of fourteen and sixteen. Hujiang won six points in the first half with twenty-two to sixteen through Feng Nianhua's two balls and Sun Baoqing's one shot.

A Difference in Mind for the Pirates. After the break, Hujiang hit two consecutive items in two minutes, one hit and then another, winning fifteen points with thirty-four to nineteen. The tense situation gradually returned to stability. The Pirates seemed to dislike the referee's bias, and they had a state of letting it go. This difference in mind led to failure.

Almost a Tie at the End. The Pirates' carelessness also led to Hujiang's relaxation. The actions of both sides were sometimes rough. The Pirates took the opportunity to advance at this time, and the score accumulated. Thirty-six to eight was only six points behind. There were still two minutes left in the game. Bernard Shigiya really added four points, only two points away. There was no one under Hujiang's basket, and Bernard's single shot failed. In a blink of an eye, the game ended, and Hujiang won with thirty-eight to thirty-six.

New Basketball Techniques (24) (Not to be) Reprinted 114

Original by Claire Burcky, Translated jointly by Zhang Guoxun and Qian Yiqin

Luuis Menzeo, the head basketball coach of Iowa State University, once broke the zone defense with the tactics recorded in this article.

However, when applying this method, the team members must be steady when receiving the ball, and they must attack with a swift and unexpected method to defeat the enemy.

Number 4 advances to the right wing of the opponent's defensive zone, then passes the ball to number 5. When number 5 is threatened by the opponent, he immediately dribbles quickly towards the free throw line, dribbles a few times, and then passes to number 3. Number 3 also rebounds and passes to number 2. If the speed of the ball is appropriate, then at this time, the only defender of numbers 1 and 2 is the opponent's left guard. At this time, if number 1 runs towards the corner, number 2 can dribble the ball towards the arc of the free throw area and shoot. If number 1 runs outside the arc of the free throw area, then number 2 can also dribble behind the defender and shoot.

Free Talk

All Citizens Should Receive Military Training 115

A couple brought a child to visit Old Man Xiang. Old Man Xiang said to them: Your good child should exercise their physique within ten years of age, so that they will be healthy in the future and be considered a citizen of Greater China! Because according to the current national crisis, judging from it, it is feared that it will cause the "Three Peoples" to govern together! One is the European people, the second is the American people, and the third is the so-called Japanese people, who will all come to bully us! Therefore, I have remembered the following important proposals.

Old Man Xiang mentioned that when he founded Aurora and Fudan, he hired instructors to teach military exercises, and students also had to practice shooting. He remembers very clearly that once, Shao Lizi fired three shots in a row and hit all three! Old Man Xiang was very happy when he talked about it. I wonder if Mr. Shao has forgotten this proud thing now?

Therefore, the reason for the proposal is not only to advocate universal conscription: because military training of children can call on citizens to have a spirit of exploration and adventure, and the energy to use their physique. So, how can the implementation be done? Briefly describe it.

The academic, industrial, and commercial circles have time in the afternoon: so from 5 PM to 7 PM, or 6 PM to 8 PM, they can hold exercises.

The agricultural sector can hold exercises in the first half of the day: because they can often get up early, as early as 5 AM to 7 AM, or 6 AM to 8 AM.

Men aged sixteen to forty have the obligation to serve in the military; those aged fifteen or sixteen, after graduating from middle school or elementary school, have the obligation to practice military exercises for one year.

Women have the obligation to practice nursing care and repairing military equipment.

In this way, the "Three Peoples" will not dare to govern China together! The important thing is implementation!

Continuing Anecdotes about Lin Sen 116

— Yangshan

丨Born as a Wireless Telegraph Student丨

A few days ago, there was an "Anecdote about Lin Sen" in Free Talk. I grew up in Rongcheng and know a lot about Chairman Lin's words and deeds. I will write down what I have seen and heard in a mess, just to imitate, not dare to compare.

Chairman Lin was originally a wireless telegraph student, but he gave up and served in the customs. "Heroes don't care about lowly origins." Foreign presidents have been tailors. I really admire the Chairman's environment and success!

He is sixty-five years old this year, and his spirit is very vigorous. He has been widowed for a long time and has no children. He built his own tomb in Guanjiang, Rongcheng, and his old home is in Shanggan Township in Inner Qili.

When the Guangdong army captured Min, he was once elected as the provincial governor. Order relied on him to maintain it. He soon gave up politics and retired to Qingzhi Temple in Guanjiang, which shows that he regarded wealth and fame as worthless.

The Chairman's official residence is in Shibanqiao, Nanjing. It is narrow and shabby, and the equipment is very simple. Except for a few boxes of calligraphy and paintings, there is nothing of value. It is said that he is quite fond of antiques, but he only seeks to be satisfied, and does not have to pay attention to quality.

He never recklessly recommends private individuals. This time when he returned to his hometown, some villagers asked him for a job. He wrote the eight characters "A gentleman is steadfast in poverty, and his career is often difficult" to encourage them, and advised them to engage in agriculture and industry to solve their livelihood.

Two Female Novel Fans 117

— Wulang

丨Influenced by Dream of the Red Chamber and A Twosome in Laughter and Tears丨

I remember Mr. Cheng Xiaoqing once told me in person that when one of his works was published in the newspaper on a daily basis, a female teacher collected these newspapers every day. One day, she accidentally lost one, and she was so angry that she did not eat that day. It can be seen that the charming power of detective novels is really not small, as great as the charming power of martial arts novels, but romantic novels are more likely to fascinate people. The following are stories of two people who are obsessed with romantic novels.

One of them, I only know her surname is Shen, because she is my neighbor. Her family calls her Miss Two. She loves to read Dream of the Red Chamber. Usually, you can hear her reciting the songs and poems of Dream of the Red Chamber in a loud voice. She got married the year before last. Still in the honeymoon of the wedding, a relative living near her husband's house sent interesting news. It turned out that one day, only a week after her marriage, she and her new husband closed the door of the new house. She lay on the bed and sobbed, crying more and more sadly, and crying louder and louder. Her parents-in-law heard the new daughter-in-law crying, and only thought that their son was bullying her in some way, so they rushed to order them to open the door, went in and asked the reason, but their son replied with a smile: "She is pretending to be Lin Daiyu, teaching me to learn from Jia Baoyu to persuade her, there is nothing else." Her parents-in-law forgave her because she was a new daughter-in-law, but they couldn't help but smile wryly. Since then, her sisters-in-law have called her "Crazy Miss."

There is also a female classmate from my former alma mater, who was fascinated by the novel "A Twosome in Laughter and Tears." This spring, she married one of my colleagues, who is a handsome young man. In her eyes, he is really comparable to Fan Jashu in "A Twosome in Laughter and Tears." She usually regards herself as He Lina. Sometimes when I go to his house, I call them "Mr. Fan" and "Miss He" as a joke. But she is really interesting. She calls me "Mr. Tao," it turns out that she also stubbornly made me play the role of Tao Bohe. After the "A Twosome in Laughter and Tears" film of the Star Company was released, I invited them to watch it twice, but the sincere and moving performances in the film made her even more fascinated. This colleague has told me secretly several times, "Your female classmate is really crazy, always complaining that I am a useless Fan Jashu, and there is no Shen Fengxi and Guan Xiugu, isn't it funny." Once, this colleague accidentally accompanied people to drink fancy wine because of socializing, but she detected it. The couple made a scene. After I learned this news, I went to persuade her, and I jokingly said, "Don't you want your Fan Jashu to have a Shen Fengxi?" She replied angrily: "Aren't Shen Fengxi and He Lina the same person?" (In the film, Hu Die plays both Shen Fengxi and He Lina.)

Poetry of Humanity 118

— Tao Zaidong

丨Makes People Startled and Horrified丨

Humanity depicts the prosperity of the city on one side, promoting the depravity of young people, and on the other side, it captures the reality of the Shaanxi disaster, expressing the difficulties of agriculture. Inserting poems in the middle makes people startled and horrified, so the poems were recited for a while. Some students came to ask about the origin of the poems. I remember two of them and describe them as follows:

Hoeing millet under the midday sun, sweat dripping onto the soil, know that the food in the plate, every grain is hard-won. This is a poem by Nie Yizhong of the Late Tang Dynasty. The poetic realm of the Late Tang Dynasty is not high, and Nie also has no poetic reputation. Because Emperor Mingzong Li Siyuan of the Later Tang Dynasty, a barbarian who claimed to be emperor, and Prime Minister Feng Dao, cited this poem in his response, intending to advise him to stop fighting and care for agriculture. Later, Sima Guang's General Mirror and Zhu Xi's Outline all adopted this passage of response, so the poem spread among the population. At that time, Feng Dao cited another poem, which said: "Selling new silk in February, selling new grain in May, treating the sores in front of you, cutting off the flesh in your heart." It also described the suffering of farmers.

"Behind vermillion gates, meat and wine rot, on the road lie frozen corpses." This is a poem by Du Gongbu in his Northern Expedition. This poem has a hundred rhymes in five words and is a masterpiece in Du's collection. The poem describes the Tianbao Rebellion and the individual's journey home, as well as his feelings and ambitions, which is now called the realist school of literature. These two sentences are angry words about the inequality of wealth and happiness, and are no less than a portrayal of Shanghai today. Those who read it without being alarmed are not human. I believe that Du is called the saint of poetry, with all kinds of beauty. Reading his poetry can lead to writing essays and novels, and writing scripts. It is not necessary to write poetry. The "Du Shi Jing Quan" is the best for compiling annual annotations of his poems.

I say this because the historical materials of our country are very rich, and literature is indeed valuable. I hope that our young people, in their spare time from science classes, may wish to choose and purchase several kinds of classics, histories, philosophers, and collections to browse and entertain, which is equivalent to reading novels and magazines. After reading a lot, they will definitely arouse interest and benefit their knowledge. I hope they will not have preconceived notions and reject them without reading. When applying them, quoting European poems and American proverbs is also good in Western languages, but how can Chinese people not be interested?

Dead End (2) 119

— Fan Yanqiao

She sang each word in a low, melodious, mournful, and well-modulated Suzhou dialect, and each word passed from the cold air to Third Aunt's eardrums, touching her heartstrings, and she heard her lower her head, silently, as if shedding tears there, because the faint moonlight shone on her teardrops, flickering with light, which Ai Gu saw, very surprised, and asked:

"Crying? Why? I won't sing anymore, so as not to make you sad."

"No! No! You sing, you sing, I accidentally thought of something, and I couldn't help but feel a little sad. I don't want to think about it, you sing!" Third Aunt quickly raised her head, stopped the remaining tears, secretly wiped them with her sleeves, and stated forcefully.

"Third Aunt, what did you think of? Would you tell me?"

"To be honest, every sentence you sing is what I have experienced, it seems. You use a needle to prick the scars I have suffered, how can I not be doubly painful. Ai Gu, remember, if you are unfortunate enough to be a woman in the next life, you would rather be a cat in a wealthy family than a daughter-in-law in a farming family." Third Aunt's head went down again, and the moonlight shone on the tear stains on her face again.

"Ah!………what!………"

Ai Gu was still a fifteen-year-old girl, not knowing the seriousness, and actually cried out loud in this quiet space that was easy for people to hear. Unfortunately, her parents-in-law and young husband all came, although there were no "sharp-tongued girls" or "short uncles," but the scolding of her parents-in-law was enough to scare her little courage.

"What the hell are you crying about in the middle of the night! What a jinx!"

"Little whore!… Are you also singing Tan Huang and crying Qiqi?!"

Two different comments from different standpoints, under the stern voice and expression, scared Third Aunt to be uneasy, and she had to stand up from the threshold, force a smile, and greet them:

"Uncle Liu!… Big Sister-in-law!… Are you done? I heard you were a little tired, so I came over here and saw your Ai Gu outside the door, afraid that she was lonely, so I chatted with her. It's ridiculous that she is really timid. I told her a story about a zombie, and she was so scared that she cried." Liu's wife said very cheerfully: "Hum… Third Aunt! No need to cover up for her! When we walked on the ridge, we still heard her singing folk songs, I don't know what she is thinking about again, and started crying. Third Aunt! It's getting late, I'll tell you tomorrow, I have a lot to say."

Third Aunt saw that she had caused trouble, so she took the opportunity to say: "See you tomorrow!" She knew in her heart that she had to leave as soon as possible, and she seemed to vaguely hear many unusual conversations, some high and some low, behind her, but she didn't want to bother to distinguish whether they were scolding her.

……………………………………………………………………

The next day, Liu's wife came to Third Aunt's house in person. Third Aunt was startled at first, but then she thought, anyway, she is a widow, not afraid of people coming to bully her, and she usually has a reputation for being "difficult to mess with," so she treated Liu's wife as an equal. In the process of serving tea, wiping the table, and dusting the bamboo building, she said a few unimportant words of small talk, and then talked about the question of "why are you here?" Liu's wife sighed first, took a sip of tea, and said:

"After you left last night, that damn girl sulked, and after a night, she is still hanging a jar of vinegar on her face today."

This month fell to 0.076 yuan, December fell to 0.074 yuan, January fell to 0.072 yuan, February fell to 0.07225 yuan, and March fell to 0.07375 yuan, falling about 0.01 yuan compared to the previous month's close. Temporary speculation again thought of raising prices, so each month gradually rebounded by over 0.01 yuan. Until the afternoon opening, the factory sales were very quiet. Also, although this month's standard was cheap, Fuxin's spot goods were still calling for 1.92 yuan with deductions, Fufeng was calling for 0.008 yuan higher than the standard, and the rest were also ranging from 0.006 to 0.004 yuan. For the distant term, both foreign customer groups also had intakes, so the market situation turned bullish. However, the pricing of Australian wheat was 3.53 yuan. The foreign firms were willing to sell, but the factories did not dare to set prices again, so although the market was slightly better, the environment was still bad. As a result, this month was 0.0125 yuan better than the previous month's end, December rose by 0.0225 yuan, January was 0.05 yuan better, February was 0.0025 yuan better, March was unchanged, and April had also opened, down 0.0005 yuan compared to the initial opening.

Silk and Tea: New Autumn Silk from Danyang Enters the Market 135

Danyang is also a silk region. Because the official government distributed improved breeds this year's autumn silkworms, and sent people to guide feeding, the harvest was still good. Because the silkworm farmers saw that the cocoon price was not high, those who reeled native silk themselves have new autumn silk entering the market. The silk quality is excellent. Unfortunately, the silk door's sales appetite is not rising, and the foreign shops and factory managers' sales prices are strangely small, resulting in low native silk opening prices. According to a letter from the production area yesterday, the highest price for new silk is only 34 yuan per 100 taels. The silkworm farmers' cocoon costs are losing money.

North-South Goods: Stone Pier Sun-Dried Meat Rises Again by 3 Yuan 139

The Stone Pier sun-dried longan meat produced in Zhangzhou had fallen to 40 yuan due to the abundant harvest of Guilin longan this year. Investigation: British Cloth Imports into China and India Increase Sharply 141

British Cotton Industry: Since the cotton mills in Manchester experienced labor unrest in the summer, there has been a decline. However, according to the latest report, the cotton cloth export trade is in good condition. It is estimated that from January to September of this year, the British cotton cloth export volume was 1.7 billion square yards, an increase of about 24% compared to last year. The reason for the increase in British cloth exports this year is that exports to the two major markets of India and China reached 115 million square yards, more than doubling compared to the same period last year. The exports to India were 465 million square yards, an increase of 5% or more compared to the same period last year. In particular, the export volume to India in September was the highest record of this year, reaching as much as 60 million square yards. This is the result of India's implementation of the new cotton cloth tax system. In addition, exports to Asia, South Africa, and India were also not small, especially the exports to Africa.
