Science

Niter "Ammonia" NH3 196

— Sheng Zhanneng

Ammonia is a very important compound in commerce. For example, liquefied ammonia is used as a refrigerant, and large amounts of ammonia are used to manufacture sodium carbonate. In agriculture, its compounds can be used as fertilizers. It also has considerable uses in medicine and industry.

Now, let's discuss its manufacture, properties, and uses in three sections:

(A) Manufacture: It can be divided into commercial production methods and laboratory production methods.

Commercial production methods: Distillation of coal is a major source of ammonia in commerce and is a very valuable by-product. Therefore, in factories that produce gas and coke on a large scale, when coal is distilled, the gas produced is washed with water to obtain a large amount of ammonia liquor. Then, the solution is separated from the tar, and then lime is added to combine with the acids, and heated, and the ammonia is driven out. (If it is passed into sulfuric acid or hydrochloric acid, ammonium sulfate or ammonium chloride can be obtained.)

Laboratory production methods:

(1) Use a mixture of slaked lime and ammonium salts (such as ammonium chloride, ammonium sulfate, etc.), and water, and heat in a still with a duct, and ammonia can be obtained.

Ca(OH)2 + 2NH4Cl → CaCl2 + 2NH4OH

NH4OH → NH3 + H2O

(2) Warming ammonia liquor also produces this gas (this gas is easily soluble in water, so it must be collected over mercury, or collected in an inverted bottle using the downward displacement of air method).

Page 18

The ammonia gas produced in the laboratory must be dried using quicklime as a drying agent.

(B) Properties:

(1) Physical properties: Ammonia is a colorless gas with a peculiar pungent odor. The density of the gas is slightly greater than that of air, and it is easily soluble in water. A 35% solution is sold as "concentrated ammonia liquor." Liquefied ammonia is often used for freezing and refrigeration. Because when ammonia in the liquid state evaporates at -33 degrees Celsius, each gram can absorb 330 calories of heat, it is an excellent refrigerant.

(2) Chemical properties: The properties of ammonia are quite unstable, and it almost completely decomposes at 700 degrees.

Ammonia can burn in pure oxygen (it does not burn in air), producing water vapor and free nitrogen. 4NH3 + 3O2 → 2N2 + 6H2O

Many oxides, when burned, can be reduced if ammonia is passed over them. 3CuO + 2NH3 → 3Cu + 3H2O + N2

Oxygen and bromine vapor can combine with the hydrogen in ammonia and cause the nitrogen to dissociate. 2NH3 + 3Cl2 → N2 + 6HCl

If a metal that can combine with nitrogen (such as magnesium) is heated in a stream of ammonia gas, the hydrogen will be substituted.

3Mg + 2NH3 → Mg3N2 + 3H2

Ammonia reacts with potassium and sodium to form amidides (compounds containing the NH2 radical), such as sodium amide NaNH2.

2NH3 + Na → 2NaNH2 + H2

At temperatures below -79.3 degrees, ammonia can also combine with water to form solid white ammonium hydroxide.

NH3 + H2O → NH4OH

The most notable property of ammonia is that it combines with acids to produce ammonium salts.

NH3 (gas) + HCl (gas) → NH4Cl (solid)

2NH3 (gas) + H2SO4 (liquid) → (NH4)2SO4 (solid)

(C) Uses: Ammonia gas itself can be used as a refrigerant and to manufacture sodium carbonate, etc., but its salts are even more important.

Ammonium sulfate: is a very important artificial fertilizer in agriculture, with a nitrogen content of 24.25% to 25%. This substance can be used to manufacture various ammonium salts, such as ammonium chloride, ammonium carbonate, ammonium hydroxide, etc. Commercially sold ammonium sulfate is usually light gray in color and often contains small amounts of acid and water.

Ammonium chloride: commonly known as sal ammoniac, is obtained by decomposing ammonium sulfate with sodium chloride (i.e., table salt) or potassium chloride. It can be purified by sublimation. It is commonly used in batteries and also in calico printing and welding. It can be used to manufacture dyes and also has considerable uses in medicine.

Ammonium bromide: is used in photography and medicine.

Ammonium fluoride: is used to etch glass.

Ammonium carbonate: can be made by heating a mixture of ammonium sulfate, chalk, and a small amount of charcoal. It is used to manufacture smelling salts, baking powder, cosmetics, and ammonium-based dyes. It is used for washing and also in medicine.

In addition, important phosphate salts include ammonium phosphate, used to manufacture artificial fertilizers, ammonium nitrate, used to manufacture explosives, and ammonium vanadate, used to manufacture black ink and for printing and dyeing fabrics, etc.

Social Improvement Discussion Group

Discussion of the "Society Improvement Discussion Group" 197

— Qian Shouyi

Recently, this newspaper's supplement has a column called "Society Improvement Discussion Group." In it, regarding all kinds of issues that we are dissatisfied with in society and consider should be improved, we have the opportunity to propose them for discussion, so as to gather everyone's opinions and decide whether to improve or abolish them. It goes without saying that the intention is very good.

The issues raised in this column are of varying sizes. Some can be improved by the ability of one person alone, such as "Improving Gift Giving," "Eliminating Bad Habits of Smoking and Drinking," "Improving Children's Sleep," etc. Some require the power of the masses to improve, such as "Abolishing Saturday Holidays," "School Fee Issues," "Reforming the Almanac," etc. However, no matter how the improvement is carried out, the problems raised for improvement are indeed worth discussing, and there is no doubt about that.

However, merely proposing discussions in this way, to let everyone know how to improve, is good, but if it is not put into practice, it is equivalent to empty talk. The reason why our country has been shouting slogans of "reform" and "overthrow" for decades, and the result is still equal to zero, is for this reason. Because in view of this point, I have further hopes for this column, and now I would like to discuss with the gentlemen who raised the questions.

In my personal opinion, the purpose of discussing social improvement issues is to truly put them into practice, so it is best not to just write on paper, or specialize in discussing large topics in the sky, and then consider it done. On the one hand, we should, based on our own observations, use the power of the newspaper to widely promote issues that should be reformed. On the other hand, we should set an example by first practicing what we can do, such as eliminating the bad habits of smoking and drinking, and then report the results and benefits we have experienced to the public. In this way, everyone will see the satisfactory results and naturally follow suit. As for social systems that cannot be fundamentally resolved at one time, we can also use flexible methods to gradually seek reform. For example, abolishing Saturday holidays is not easy to change at once due to being stuck in habits, but we can use this time to do other work. As long as everyone practices in this way, is it not equivalent to not taking a holiday? After a long time, this habit can be abolished. Only when discussion and practice are carried out simultaneously like this, is there meaning, value, and is it not a waste of everyone's thoughts.

The improvement of society is the happiness of the masses, and this mission is borne by everyone. Therefore, although I am uneducated, I dare to contribute a little opinion without considering my own shallowness. If you gentlemen think that even the humble opinions are worth adopting, I hope that we will work together to implement them.

A Corner of Society

The Game of Money 198

— Tian Fang

丨One of the Street Scenes丨

Old Chen, the coppersmith, walked out of the company's accounting office happily, holding this month's salary – ten silver dollars. He thought to himself, his wife once said: When you get your salary, you have to buy a piece of clothing for your son, but what's enough with this little money! Six dollars for rent, three dollars owed to the rice shop, and four dimes to be returned to Li Mazi, and you have to buy firewood and salt... Ah, what's enough with this little money! He thought, blankly stepping onto the asphalt road.

Four dimes for a dollar... Come win money, everyone..., a burst of drawn-out voices escaped from a large, dark crowd beside the road. At the same time, one dime went in, two dimes went in, a chorus of silver dimes.

What trick is it again? A great consciousness urged him to take a closer look.

This was a gambling stall. A wooden board table was decorated with red and green dots, arranged into heaven, earth, man, and me, four cards. The table was even pasted with two red paper slogans, "To gamble, you must think carefully, look at the cards to divide winning and losing," which were considered the gambler's slogans! The onlookers included those in short clothes and those in long gowns, men and women. Hundreds and thousands of eyes were focused on a small box on the table. The fate of these many people betting money all depended on this square inch of bamboo. In this opening and changing, copper coins were constantly moving.

Old Chen, the coppersmith, watched blankly. The skinny man in short clothes next to him won every bet. His four-dime capital had already won more than five dollars. The tall man across from him was not bad either, winning two or three dollars. He thought to himself, it's really a lucky thing. At this time, the sound of "four dimes for a dollar" and the sound of silver dollars were constantly echoing. What a tempting sound, it moved Old Chen's heart, making him involuntarily pull out the remaining two dimes in his pocket, and follow the skinny man丨he trusted his skills丨to bet on the "heaven" card.

"Four dimes minimum!" said the person at the stall. The two dimes were finally returned to his own hand, but this time, he happened to open his eyes and watch the skinny man win another dollar. Endless frustration aroused his greatest determination. He solemnly stuffed the silver dollar he earned with his blood and sweat, betting four dimes on the table. This was the first time ever, and he actually won a dollar, which made him very grateful for the skinny man's hint. The addition of a dollar to his pocket surpassed the price of a day's labor. How joyful it should be! He thought, the money for the child's clothes is there. But the human heart is insatiable, shouldn't he bet again, so even the money for oil and sauce will be available? He thought. But the reality was never as beautiful as the ideal. Four dimes were rolled back to the dealer's side again, even the skinny man was frustrated. Things were really not ordinary.

One bet after another, the bottom of his pocket gradually lightened, and his worries gradually increased. Feeling in his pocket, there were only two dollars left. He didn't want to leave, but what would happen if he didn't leave? He was lost, and lost all faith.

If I don't win this time, I won't gamble anymore! The skinny man, his comrade, put all three dollars in his hand on the line, looked at him and said. He had the air of burning his boats.

Yes, let's give it a shot! Excitement jumped into his heart, and he threw in the same amount. But unfortunately, willpower did not triumph over reality. Ten dollars were all recorded in the dealer's account for today's income. He went crazy, as if waking up from a big dream. He remembered everything... rent... debts to the rice shop... the child's clothes... He wanted to grab back the money he had lost, but for what reason? He went straight to the side of the room, and they would say he was a criminal, a thief. However, what reason did they have to take my money? His chaotic thoughts finally forced him to leave the gambling stall in a daze.

Four dimes for a dollar... the drawn-out voice still did not lose its seductive power. The second gambler was just beginning to follow in Old Chen's footsteps.

School Scene

Eccentric Person (?) 199

— Ke Bo

One morning, many anonymous slogans were found on the walls of our school. They were painted with an ugly potato and a few crooked words: What kind of bookworm, eccentric person!... After reading it, I was really baffled, and couldn't figure it out for a while.

Later, I learned that this was a slogan alluding to a student with a shaved head.

I still don't quite understand, what's the big deal with shaving one's head like a monk? Why make such a fuss? Comparing a monk's head to a potato, is it an insult? No, I think it's just a boring act! The student with the monk's head is a freshman. He never pays attention to dressing up. His rough black face never seems to have anything applied to it. A set of old student clothes, the sleeves of which are almost the same size as his feet. He wears a pair of Chaplin-style leather shoes, the heels of which are almost gone. All of this, all of this is his eternal mark. Studying in the fashionable modern student world like this, he is sure to make people look at him differently. However, he can't catch up with others in the pursuit of fashion, but he is already many steps ahead of others in his studies.

In the morning, the students are all dreaming sweet dreams. When there is only a little light that is not enough to read, he puts on a blanket, drags his wooden clogs, and runs to the grass to recite his monk scriptures. When it gets light, the students on the grass gradually increase, but he squats alone in the dormitory, studying hard.

Usually in the library, on the lawn, under the shade of trees, anyone can see him alone with a book and a pen, reading. Sometimes he is seen looking up and mumbling what he is reading, sometimes he is seen staring at a grass and a tree in a daze. Playful people see him and call out his nickname, "Potato"... but he seems not to hear it, neither angry nor showing any expression.

On Sundays and holidays, I have bumped into him several times reading in the deep paths of the park. If you greet him sincerely, he will at most return a bow and a smile. People have never seen him smile, and it seems that his life lacks the element of laughter.

He is very diligent. He washes his own clothes. As for watching movies and buying snacks, I don't think he does that. At most, it's only once or twice every six months.

Like this, he is indeed an eccentric person in the modern, fashionable, so-called advanced student world. But I always hope that more like him will be produced.

Anecdotes

Interesting Plaques 200

— Ya Shi

Once I was returning from ×× town, and happened to pass behind my cousin's Wancun. I took the opportunity to visit his house. As I was about to step into his study, I saw him holding a plaque in both hands, instructing a servant as if he was about to send it somewhere. When he saw me, he immediately smiled, shook hands, and exchanged polite words, which need not be said. The servant also stood by, waiting for his instructions. At this time, I looked at the plaque, which read, "Congratulations to the Newly Appointed Director of the ×× Department of ××," and below it read, "Respectfully Offered by Brother ××." Only the middle part was truly peculiar, it read "Bin Ka Jian Ni" four magnificent characters. After reading it, I was really at a loss, and asked him what it meant. He gave a cold laugh and calmly said to me, "This newly appointed director was my classmate for several years. His father used to be a ×× adjutant under the command of the ×× warlord. Once, this warlord and another ×× warlord fought for power, and unfortunately, they were defeated. Soldiers scattered everywhere. His old man also took this opportunity to loot civilian property while the fire was raging. He never served as an official again, and returned to his hometown to enjoy his great fortune. Now he has opened two opium dens in the ×× trading port, which is very impressive. A few days ago, he spent 10,000 sinful silver dollars to buy this official position. Is it wrong or not for me to send him a plaque with such words?" At this time, I just agreed casually, and asked him to explain it to me. He continued to say to me, "If you really want to hear the meaning of these four characters, it is quite accurate. If you ask about his talent, he is neither cultured nor martial. Putting the two characters 'culture' and 'martial' together makes the character 'Bin'. If you ask about his ambition, it is neither up nor down. Putting the two characters 'up' and 'down' together makes the character 'Ka'. If you ask about his ability, it is neither small nor big. Putting the two characters 'small' and 'big' together makes the character 'Jian'. If you talk about his personality, he is really not like a human, nor like a ghost (which can be compared to the common saying in the countryside, 'half-cooked red millet'). Putting the two characters 'human' and 'ghost' together makes the character 'Ni'. My brother, I have compiled these four characters 'Bin Ka Jian Ni' into a sentence to send to him, isn't he worthy of it?" When I heard him say this, I finally opened my confused gourd, and couldn't help but burst into a miserable laugh.

They are quite simple and durable, and the fashion is temporary. The Zhen Shan Mei Store at 1237 Zhonghua Road, South Xiaoximen, has this kind of fabric for sale. It is said that the prices are very low.
